[23/04/25, 11:28:44‚ÄØAM] CM Jagdish-CREA(I) VP: üìç *IMPORTANT: MEMBERSHIP NOTICE ‚Äì DUAL MEMBERSHIP - CREA (I)* 

CREA (I) is one of the largest Real Estate Associations in the country and we are proud of our Members and their Identity at CREA (I). 

In order to simplify and streamline the membership process within CREA (I) and NAR India, from FY 25-26 , it is mandatory that a member (old or new) of CREA (I) cannot be a member of any other association in Bangalore which is also a member of NAR India. This will ensure that issue of Dual NAR India membership is completely avoided.

[25/04/25, 12:35:59‚ÄØPM] CM Jagdish-CREA(I) VP: üìç*IMPORTANT: MEMBERSHIP NOTICE ‚Äì DUAL MEMBERSHIP - CREA (I)*

CREA (I) is one of the largest Real Estate Associations in the country and we are proud of our Members and their Identity at CREA (I). 

In order to simplify and streamline the membership process within CREA (I) and NAR India, from FY 25-26 , it is mandatory that a member (old or new) of CREA (I) cannot be a member of any other association in Bangalore which is also a member of NAR India. This will ensure that issue of Dual NAR India membership is completely avoided. Please note this is applicable to Individual & Company Memberships and also to Affiliate Non Member individuals and companies. 

Please note Non compliance to above may lead to suspension or cancellation of membership with CREA (I).

For any clarification please reach out to our Membership Committee

Regards

 *Managing Committee* 
 *CREA (I)*
